-- insert na Forums_Instructors
INSERT INTO platforma.Forums_Instructors(ForumId, InstructorId, Comment, DateComment)
SELECT (random() * 8 + 1)::integer as ForumId, i.Id, 'I  am instructor and I love this topic', (now() - random()*interval '15 days')::date
FROM platforma.instructors i
WHERE i.Id % 2 = 0;


-- insert na Forums_Students 1/2
INSERT INTO platforma.Forums_Students(ForumId, StudentId, Comment, DateComment)
SELECT (random() * 8 + 1)::integer as ForumId, s.Id, 'I  am a student and I love this topic', (now() - random()*interval '15 days')::date
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 2 = 0;


-- insert na Forums_Students 2/2
INSERT INTO platforma.Forums_Students(ForumId, StudentId, Comment, DateComment)
SELECT (random() * 8 + 1)::integer as ForumId, s.Id, 'I am a student and this is great!!!', (now() - random()*interval '15 days')::date
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 3 = 0;

FROM platforma.courses c
WHERE c.name LIKE '%Web%' OR c.name LIKE '%JavaScript%' OR c.name LIKE '%Angular%'
OR c.name LIKE '%React%' OR c.name LIKE '%JS%' OR c.name LIKE '%PHP%' OR c.name LIKE '%MVC%';

-- trigger za insert na bought_courses ------------------------------------------------------------
-- ova mi sluzhi za da im se namali brojot na tokenite so koi shto kupuvaat kurs
-- primer ako liceto X ima 30 tokeni i kupi kurs shto chini 10 tokeni, ke ima 20 tokeni.

CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION platforma.tokens_bought_courses() RETURNS TRIGGER AS $tokens_update$
   BEGIN
      UPDATE platforma.Students s
       SET tokens = tokens - (SELECT p.price FROM platforma.prices p WHERE p.courseid = new.CourseId)
      WHERE s.id = new.studentId;
      RETURN NEW;
   END;
$tokens_update$ LANGUAGE plpgsql;

CREATE TRIGGER platforma.Trigger_Tokens_Bought_Courses
    AFTER INSERT ON platforma.Bought_Courses
    FOR EACH ROW
    EXECUTE PROCEDURE platforma.tokens_bought_courses();
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------


-- insert na Bought_Courses x1
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x2
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 3 = 0;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x3
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 5 = 0;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x4
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 10 = 0 AND s.tokens > 12;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x5
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 15 = 0 AND s.tokens > 12;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x6
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 20 = 0 AND s.tokens > 12;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x7
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12;


-- dopolnuvanje na tokenite na studentite (za da imam povekje zapisi vo tabelata Bought_Courses)
UPDATE platforma.students
set tokens = tokens + 150;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x8
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s;


-- insert na Bought_Courses x9
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12 and s.Id % 3 = 0;

-- insert na Bought_Courses x10 (20 pati)

FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12;

-- insert na Bought_Courses x10 (20 pati)
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12;

-- insert na Bought_Courses x10 (20 pati)

FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12;

-- insert na Bought_Courses x10 (20 pati)
INSERT INTO platforma.Bought_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateBought)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 125 + 1)::integer as CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateBought
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.tokens > 12;

-- insert na Watched_Courses, pochnati no nedovrsheni
INSERT INTO platforma.Watched_Courses(StudentId, CourseId)
SELECT bc.StudentId, bc.CourseId
FROM platforma.Bought_Courses bc
WHERE (bc.StudentId % 2 = 0 OR bc.StudentId % 3 = 0)
AND bc.StudentId % 15 != 0;


-- insert na Watched_Courses, zavrsheni
INSERT INTO platforma.Watched_Courses(StudentId, CourseId, DateFinished)
SELECT bc.StudentId, bc.CourseId, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date
FROM platforma.Bought_Courses bc
WHERE bc.StudentId % 15 = 0;


-- insert na Course_Review
INSERT INTO platforma.Course_Review(StudentId, CourseId, Grade, DateReview)
SELECT wc.StudentId, wc.CourseId, (random() * 5 + 5)::integer as Grade, (now() - random()*interval '3 months')::date as DateReview
FROM platforma.Watched_Courses wc
WHERE wc.StudentId % 4 = 0;


-- insert na Certificates
INSERT INTO platforma.Certificates(StudentId, CourseId, DateCertified)
SELECT wc.StudentId, wc.CourseId, wc.DateFinished as DateCertified
FROM platforma.Watched_Courses wc
WHERE wc.DateFinished IS NOT NULL;


-- insert na Course_Recommendations 1/2
INSERT INTO platforma.Course_Recommendations(student1id, student2id, courseid)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 5928 + 1)::integer as Student2, (random() * 19 + 1)::integer as CourseId
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 7 = 0;


-- insert na Course_Recommendations 2/2
INSERT INTO platforma.Course_Recommendations(student1id, student2id, courseid)
SELECT s.Id, (random() * 5928 + 1)::integer as Student2, (random() * 19 + 1)::integer as CourseId
FROM platforma.students s
WHERE s.Id % 6 = 0;
